@create Self CharGen Commands
@create Chargen
@create Data Dictionary

@create Stat Reference
@create XP Gain System
@create XP Gain Database
@create XP Cost Database
@create XP Spend Log

&C.+MYSTAT_TEMPLATE Self CharGen Commands=$+mystat/template *:@pemit %#=[alert(Chargen)] [if(not(hasattr(%#, _cglock)), [setq(p, pmatch+(%#))][setq(w, u(#234/f.find-sheet, %qp))][switch(0, t(%qp), Player Not Found., not(hasattr(%qw, _bio.template)), You already have a template. +mystat/wipe to erase your stats and start over., [setq(v, iter(%0, statvalidate(template, %i0), ., .))][not(match(%qv, #-*, .))], One or more templates did not validate., [setq(l, setunion(iter(%qv, filter(#234/filter.stat-allowed-for-template, iter(lattr([u(#234/d.data-dictionary)]/default.*), rest(%i0, .)), , , %i0), .), ))][header(Setup [name(%qp)] as a [edit(%qv, ., /)])] %r%b [ansi(h, Sheet Location)]: %qs %r%b [ansi(h, Template)]: %qv[null(set(%qw, _BIO.TEMPLATE:%qv))] %r%b [iter(%ql, [ansi(h, ulocal([u(#234/d.stat-funcs)]/f.statname-workhorse, rest(%i0, .)))]: [get([u(#234/d.data-dictionary)]/default.%i0)][null(set(%qw, _%i0:[get([u(#234/d.data-dictionary)]/default.%i0)]))], , %r %b)] %r[footer(+sheet [name(%qp)])])], Your stats are already submitted for review%, you cannot change them. If you do not currently have a job in with staff please +request to have chargen unlocked.)]
&C.+MYSTAT/SET Self CharGen Commands=$+mystat/set *=*:@pemit %#=[alert(Chargen)] [if(not(isapproved(%#)), if(not(hasattr(%#, _cglock)), setstat(%#/%0, %1), Your stats are already submitted for approval%, you cannot change them. If you do not currently have a job open with staff please +request to have chargen unlocked.), You have been approved%, you cannot change your stats.)]
&C.+MYSTAT/DONE Self CharGen Commands=$+mystat/done:@pemit %#=[alert(Chargen)] [if(not(isapproved(%#)), if(not(hasattr(%#, _cglock)), if(hasattr(%#, _bio.template), Submitting stats to staff. Please add anything you were unable to set and any incentives to the generated +myjob.[set(%#, _cglock:1)][trigger(#15/trig_create, %#, u(#15/fn_find-bucket,APPS), 2, Stats - [name(%#)], [name(%#)] has finished chargen as a [getstat(%#/Template)] and needs to be checked over.)], You have no stats set to submit to staff.), Your stats are already locked for review. If you do not currently have an app job in please +Request to have chargen unlocked.), You are already approved.)]
&C.+MYSTAT/UNLOCK Self CharGen Commands=$+mystat/unlock *:@pemit %#=[alert(Chargen)] [if(not(isstaff(%#)), Only staff can use this command., if(pmatch+(%0), Clearing [name(pmatch+(%0))]'s stat lock.[set(pmatch+(%0), _cglock:)], I cannot find %0.))]
&C.+MYSTAT/WIPE Self CharGen Commands=$+mystat/wipe*:@pemit %#=[alert(Chargen)] [if(not(isapproved(%#)), [if(not(hasattr(%#, _cglock)), [setq(0, before(%0, =))][setq(1, after(%0, =))][case(0, t(setr(p, pmatch+(%#))), Player Not Found., hasattr(setr(w, u(#234/f.find-sheet, %qp)), _bio.template), You have no stats to wipe., comp(%q1, YES), [setq(l, edit(iter([u([u(#234/d.stat-funcs)]/d.type-search-order)] [u([u(#234/d.stat-funcs)]/d.type-specials)], iter(lattr(%qw/_%i0.*), rest(%i0, _))), BIO.TEMPLATE, @@(null)))][header(Wiping Your Sheet)] %r%b [iter(BIO.TEMPLATE %ql, [ansi(h, u([u(#234/d.stat-funcs)]/f.statname workhorse, rest(%i0, .)))]: [get(%qw/_%i0)] [null(set(%qw, _%i0:))], , %r %b)] %r[footer(Sheet Wiped)], [ansi(g, >> Are you%b, hgu, absolutely sure, g, %byou want to wipe your sheet? <<)] %rIf so%, type: [ansi(h, +mystat/wipe me=YES)])], Your stats are already submitted for approval%, you cannot change them. If you do not currently have a job in with staff please +request to have chargen unlocked.)], You have been approved%, you cannot wipe your sheet.)]
@set Self CharGen Commands=INHERIT
@set Self CharGen Commands=SAFE !HALT

&D.DATA-DICTIONARY Chargen=#231
&D.STAT-FUNCTIONS Chargen=#233
&F.LIST-STATS-TAGS Chargen=filter([u(d.stat-functions)]/fil.list-stats-tags, rest(edit(lattr(%0/_%1.*), %b_, %b), _), , , %2, not(strmatch(%3, or)))
&FIL.LIST-STATS-TAGS Chargen=ulocal([u(d.stat-functions)]/f.hastag?.workhorse,ulocal([u(d.stat-functions)]/f.statpath-without-instance, %0), %1, %2)
&F.POINTS.CATEGORY Chargen=[setq(l, u(f.list-stats-tags, %0, %1, %2))][setr(s, ladd(iter(%ql, [setr(b, first(u(%0/_%i0), .))])))]
&F.ALLOCATED.ATTRIBUTES Chargen=iter(mental physical social, sub(u(f.points.category, %0, attribute, %i0), 3), , /)
&F.ALLOCATED.SKILLS Chargen=iter(mental physical social, u(f.points.category, %0, skill, %i0), , /)
&F.ALLOCATED.SPECIALTIES Chargen=[setq(l, ulocal(f.list-stats-tags, %0, skill, mental.physical.social, or))][setq(s, iter(%ql, lattr(%0/_%i0.*)))][iter(revwords(u(%0/_bio.template), .), [setq(f, u(f.allocated.specialties.%i0, %0, %qs))][iter(%qf, iter(%i0, setq(s, remove(%qs, %i0))), `, @@)], ., @@)]%qs[if(%qf, `%qf)]
&F.ALLOCATED.MERITS Chargen=[ladd([ulocal(f.points.category, %0, merit, *)] [ulocal(f.points.category, %0, rite, *)] [iter(revwords(u(%0/_bio.template), .), ulocal(f.allocated.merits.%i0, %0), .)] [iter(lattr(%0/_merit.*.*), -[first(u(%0/%i0), .)])])]/[max(0, mul(sub(ulocal(f.points.category, %0, advantage, power level), 1), 5))]
&F.ALLOCATED.MERITS.CHANGELING Chargen=[if(gte(first(u(%0/_merit.mantle_%([u(%0/_bio.court)]%)), .), 1), -1)] [iter([u(%0/_bio.kith)].[u(%0/_bio.seeming)], -[u(f.allocated.merits.changeling.%i0, %0)], .)]
&F.ALLOCATED.SPECIALTIES.CHANGELING Chargen=localize([setq(l, %1)][setq(k, iter(u(%0/_bio.kith), u(f.allocated.specialties.changeling.%i0, %0, ), .))][iter(%qk, setq(l, remove(%ql, %i0)))][setq(s, iter(u(%0/_bio.seeming), u(f.allocated.specialties.changeling.%i0, %0, ), .))][iter(%qs, setq(l, remove(%ql, %i0)))][setq(c, first(iter(athletics brawl stealth, grab(%ql, _skill.%i0.*))))]%qc`%qs`%qk)
&F.ALLOCATED.SPECIALTIES.CHANGELING.BEAST Chargen=first(lattr(%0/_skill.animal_ken.*))
&F.PTS-VALID?.ATTRIBUTES Chargen=[setq(a, sort(u(f.allocated.attributes, %0), n, /))][and([eq(first(%qa, /), 3)], [eq(extract(%qa, 2, 1, /), 4)], [eq(last(%qa, /), 5)])]
&F.PTS-VALID?.SKILLS Chargen=[setq(a, sort(u(f.allocated.skills, %0), n, /))][and([eq(first(%qa, /), 4)], [eq(extract(%qa, 2, 1, /), 7)], [eq(last(%qa, /), 11)])]
&F.PTS-VALID?.SPECIALTIES Chargen=localize([setq(s, u(f.allocated.specialties, %0))][land([eq(words(first(%qs, `)), 3)] [iter(u(%0/_bio.template), udefault(f.pts-valid?.specialties.%i0, 1, %0, %qs), .)])])
&F.PTS-VALID?.MERITS Chargen=[eq(ladd(u(f.allocated.merits, %0), /), [if(israce(%0, human), 7, 10)])]
&F.ALLOCATED.CONTRACTS Chargen=add(u(f.points.category, %0, contract, *), u(f.points.category, %0, goblin_contract, *))
&F.PTS-VALID?.CONTRACTS Chargen=[eq(u(f.allocated.contract, %0), 6)]
&F.PREREQUSITE.CG-ONLY Chargen=if(not(and(hastag?(rest(%1, .), chargen-only), isapproved(%0))), 1, #-1 CHARGEN ONLY STATS CANNOT BE GAINED AFTER APPROVAL)
&F.PREREQUSITE.TEMPLATE Chargen=localize([setq(s, ulocal([u(d.stat-functions)]/f.statpath-without-instance, %1))][setq(t, setinter(lcstr(u([u(d.data-dictionary)]/bio.template)), lcstr(u([u(d.data-dictionary)]/tags.[rest(%qs, _)])), .))][if(t(%qt), if(t(setinter(lcstr(u(%0/_bio.template)), lcstr(%qt), .)), 1, #-1 Character Template Not Allowed For This Stat), 1)])
&F.PREREQUSITE.OTHER Chargen=localize([setq(i, before(rest(%1, %(), %)))][setq(s, ulocal([u(d.stat-functions)]/f.statpath-without-instance, %1))][setq(p, ulocal([u(d.data-dictionary)]/prerequisite.[rest(%qs, _)], %0, %qi, %2))][case(0, comp(%qp, ), 1, %qp, #-1 [u([u(d.data-dictionary)]/prereq-text.[rest(%qs, _)])], 1)])
&F.STATCHECK Chargen=localize([setq(s, ulocal([u(d.stat-functions)]/f.statpath-without-instance, rest(%1, _)))][setq(c, udefault([u(d.data-dictionary)]/class.%qs, numeric))][setq(v, case(%qc, numeric, first(u(%0/%1), .), u(%0/%1)))][setq(t, case(1, strmatch(%1, _*.*.*), u(f.statcheck.substat, %0, %1, %2), strmatch(get([u(d.data-dictionary)]/%qs), %[*%]*), u(f.statcheck.derived, %0, %1), strmatch(%qc, list), u(f.statcheck.list, %qs, %qv, %2), u(f.statcheck.normal, %1, %qs, %qv, %2)))][if(t(%qt), 1, %qt)].[iter(cg-only template other, u(f.prerequsite.%i0, %0, %1, %2), , .)])
&F.STATCHECK.NORMAL Chargen=localize([setq(t, if(hasattr([u(d.data-dictionary)], %1), 1, #-1 Stat not found))][setq(t, if(and(t(%qt), strmatch(%0, _*.*_(*))), [setq(i, edit(strip(rest(%0, %(), %)), _, %b))][setq(d, extract(get([u(d.data-dictionary)]/%1), 2, 1, |))][case(1, t(member(%qd, *)), 1, and(member(%qd, #), isint(%qi)), 1, t(match(%qd, %qi, .)), 1, #-1 Instance is not valid %(%qi%))], %qt))][setq(v, case(1, and(isnum(%2), t(%3)), add(%2, %3), t(%3), %3, %2))][if(t(%qt), ulocal([u(d.stat-functions)]/f.statvalidate.workhorse, %1, %qv), %qt)])
&F.STATCHECK.DERIVED Chargen=if(or(isint(first(u(%0/%1), .)), strmatch(lcstr(get([u(d.data-dictionary)]/class.[rest(ulocal([u(d.stat-functions)]/f.statpath-without-instance, %1), _)])), string)), 1, #-1 Derived stat is non-numeric)
&F.STATCHECK.SUBSTAT Chargen=localize(case(0, and(isint(setr(t, first(u(%0/[extract(%1, 1, 2, .)]), .))), gt(%qt, 0)), #-1 Substat cannot be set if main stat is non-numeric, or(not(strmatch(%1, _skill.*)), eq(add(u(%0/%1), %2), 1)), #-1 Specialty substats value are 1, 1))
&F.TEMP-OUTPUT-CHECKSTATS Chargen=[setq(0, pmatch+(%0))][setq(b, u(f.badstats, %q0))][iter(%qb, >> [u([u(d.stat-functions)]/f.statname-workhorse, rest(%i0, .))]: [itemize(trim(iter(u(cg/f.statcheck, %q0, %i0), if(not(%i0), [titlestr(rest(%i0))]|), ., @@), b, |), |)], , %r)]

&F.ALLOCATED.SPECIALTIES.CHANGELING.DAITYA Chargen=first(lattr(%0/_skill.weaponry.*))

&F.ALLOCATED.SPECIALTIES.CHANGELING.NIGHTSINGER Chargen=first(lattr(%0/_skill.expression.*))
&F.ALLOCATED.MERITS.CHANGELING.INCUBUS Chargen=u(f.allocated.merits.changeling.succubus, %0)
&F.ALLOCATED.MERITS.CHANGELING.PAMARINDO Chargen=first(u(%0/_merit.iron_stomach), .)
&F.ALLOCATED.MERITS.CHANGELING.SUCCUBUS Chargen=if(t(first(u(%0/_merit.striking_looks), .)), 2)
&C.TEST.SET Chargen=$^([a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z\s\(\)]*\.?[a-zA-Z\s]*[a-zA-Z])\s*(([\+-=])\s*(.*))?$:@pemit %#=[setq(s, u([u(d.stat-functions)]/f.statpath-without-instance, if(t(setr(s, statpath(%#/%1))), %qs, statpath(%1))))][setq(n, statname(rest(%qs, .)))][setq(e, case(1, isapproved(%#), #-1 You're already approved., not(hasattr(%#, _bio.template)), #-1 You don't have a sheet set up., strmatch(%qs, skill.*.*), [null(objeval(#13, setstat(%#/%1, 1, override)))]Set Specialty of [rest(%qn, .)] for [first(%qn, .)],t(match(+ -, %3)), objeval(#13, shiftstat(%#/%1, %3%4)), and(not(comp(%4, )), eq(words(setr(v, first(u([u(d.data-dictionary)]/%qs), |)), .), 1)), objeval(#13, setstat(%#/%1, %qv)), objeval(#13, setstat(%#/%1, %4))))][if(t(%qe), Confirmed: %qe, Error: [titlestr(rest(%qe))])]
@set Chargen/C.TEST.SET = regexp
&C.TEST.UNSET Chargen=$^!([a-zA-Z][a-zA-Z\s\(\)]*\.?[a-zA-Z\s]*[a-zA-Z])?$:@pemit %#=Unset :: <stat>: %1
@set Chargen/C.TEST.UNSET = regexp
&F.BADSTAT? Chargen=not(land(u(f.statcheck, %1, %0), .))

&F.ALLOCATED.GIFTS Chargen=localize([setq(e, u(f.list-stats-tags, %0, gift, *))][setq(t, u(f.list-stats-tags, %0, gift, get(%0/_bio.tribe)))][setq(a, u(f.list-stats-tags, %0, gift, get(%0/_bio.auspice)))][setq(o, setdiff(%qe, %qa %qt))][setq(r, first(udefault(%0/_merit.rituals, 0), .))][setq(i, land(iter(%qe, [setq(g, edit(get(%0/_%i0), ., %b))][eq(ladd(%qg), ladd(lnum(1, last(sort(%qg)))))])))][setq(e, ladd([iter(%qe, words(u(%0/_%i0), .))] %qr))][setq(t, ladd(iter(%qt, words(u(%0/_%i0), .))))][setq(a, ladd(iter(%qa, words(u(%0/_%i0), .))))][setq(o, ladd(iter(%qo, words(u(%0/_%i0), .))))]%qe (Auspice: %qa - Tribe: %qt - Other: %qo - Rituals: %qr)%, Ordered: [if(t(%qi), Yes, No)] )

&_VALUE Data Dictionary=case(u(_class, %1), numeric, first(u(_value_full, %0, %1), .), u(_value_full, %0, %1))
&_AT_LEAST Data Dictionary=gte(add(u(_value, %0, %1), %3), %2)
&_AT_LEAST_ALL Data Dictionary=land(iter(%1, u(_at_least, %0, first(%i0, :), rest(%i0, :))))
&_AT_LEAST_ONE Data Dictionary=lor(iter(%1, u(_at_least, %0, first(%i0, :), rest(%i0, :))))
&_AT_LEAST_STAT Data Dictionary=localize([setq(t, trim(first(edit(%2, -, +-), +)))][setq(a, iter(rest(edit(edit(%2, -%b, -), -, %b+-), +), %i0, +))][u(_at_least, %0, %1, ladd([u(_value, %0, %qt)] %qa), %3)])
&_AT_MOST Data Dictionary=lte(add(u(_value, %0, %1), %3), %2)
&_AT_MOST_ALL Data Dictionary=land(iter(%1, u(_at_most, %0, first(%i0, :), rest(%i0, :))))
&_AT_MOST_ONE Data Dictionary=lor(iter(%1, u(_at_most, %0, first(%i0, :), rest(%i0, :))))
&_AT_MOST_STAT Data Dictionary=localize([setq(t, trim(first(edit(%2, -, +-), +)))][setq(a, iter(rest(edit(edit(%2, -%b, -), -, %b+-), +), %i0, +))][u(_at_most, %0, %1, ladd([u(_value, %0, %qt)] %qa), %3)])
&_IS Data Dictionary=strmatch(%2, if(t(%3), %3, u(_value, %0, %1)))
&_IS_NOT Data Dictionary=not(u(_is, %0, %1, %2, %3))
&_IS_ONE_OF Data Dictionary=t(match(%2, u(_value, %0, %1), .))
&_IS_NONE_OF Data Dictionary=not(u(_is_one_of, %0, %1, %2))
&_HAS Data Dictionary=t(u(_value, %0, %1))
&_HAS_NOT Data Dictionary=not(u(_value, %0, %1))
&_HAS_ONE_OF Data Dictionary=lor(iter(%1, u(_has, %0, %i0)))
&_HAS_NONE_OF Data Dictionary=not(u(_has_one_of, %0, %1))
&_HAS_ALL_OF Data Dictionary=land(iter(%1, u(_has, %0, %i0)))
&_MIN_OF Data Dictionary=min(u(_value, %0, first(%1)), if(dec(words(rest(%1))), u(_min_of, %0, rest(%1)), u(_value, %0, rest(%1))))
&_MAX_OF Data Dictionary=max(u(_value, %0, first(%1)), if(dec(words(rest(%1))), u(_max_of, %0, rest(%1)), u(_value, %0, rest(%1))))

&F.FIND-PLAYERS XP Gain System=search(eplayer=u(f.is_approved?, ##))
&F.IS_APPROVED? XP Gain System=isapproved(%0)
&TR.CYCLE.PROCESS-AND-LOG XP Gain System=&log.[secs()] [v(d.database)]=[iter(%0, %i0|[ulocal(f.cycle.process-player, %i0)])]
&F.CYCLE.PROCESS-PLAYER XP Gain System=[setq(b, get(%0/_special.xp))][setq(a, [add(first(%qb, .), u(d.xp.per-cycle))].[rest(%qb, .)])][if(not(comp(setr(s, set(%0, _special.xp:%qa)), )), %qb|%qa, %qs)]
@DescFormat XP Gain System=%0%r[u(f.log)]%r[footer(Report)]
&TR.CYCLE XP Gain System=@trigger %!/tr.cycle.process-and-log=[u(f.find-players)]; @trigger %!/tr.cycle.process-and-log-freezered=[u(f.find-frozen)]; @trigger [u(d.xp-frob)]/trig.plot-log-clear; &d.time.stamp %!=[secs()]; @trigger %!/tr.wait
&TR.WAIT XP Gain System=@if [not(hasattr(%!, d.time.stamp))]={&d.time.stamp %!=[secs()]}; @wait/until [add(v(d.time.stamp), v(d.time.cycle))]={@trigger %!/tr.cycle}
@Startup XP Gain System=@trigger %!/tr.wait
&F.CYCLE.TEST XP Gain System=--> &log.[secs()] [v(d.database)]=[setq(s, u(f.find-players))][if(t(%qs), iter(%qs, %i0|[u(f.cycle.process-player, %i0)]))]
&D.TIME.STAMP XP Gain System=1387333564
&F.LOG XP Gain System=Standard XP Log: %r%b Most Recent Log ([words(setr(0, lattr([u(d.database)]/log.*)))] Total): [lcstr(setr(1, first(revwords(sort(%q0)))))]%r%b People: [words(setr(2, u([u(d.database)]/%q1)))]%r%b Errors: [words(graball(%q2, *|#-*))]%rFrozen XP Log: %r%b Most Recent Frozen ([words(setr(0, lattr([u(d.database)]/frozen.*)))] Total): [lcstr(setr(1, first(revwords(sort(%q0)))))]%r%b People: [words(setr(2, u([u(d.database)]/%q1)))]%r%b Errors: [words(graball(%q2, *|#-*))]%rThis Week's Plot XP: %r%b People: [words(setr(0, lattr([u(d.database)]/plot.extra.*)))]%r%b XP: [ladd(iter(%q0, first(get([u(d.database)]/%i0), |)))]%rLast Week's Plot XP: %r%b Log: [setq(0, lattr([u(d.database)]/plot.log.*))][lcstr(setr(1, first(revwords(sort(%q0)))))]%r%b People: [words(setr(2, get([u(d.database)]/%q1)))]%r%b XP: [ladd(iter(%q2, extract(%i0, 2, 1, |)))]%rTotal Previous Plot XP: %r%b Num Logs: [words(%q0)]%r%b People: [words(iter(setq(1, iter(%q0, get([u(d.database)]/%i0))), first(%i0, |)), )]%r%b XP: [ladd(iter(%q1, extract(%i0, 1, 2, |)))]
&TR.CYCLE.PROCESS-AND-LOG-FREEZERED XP Gain System=&frozen.[secs()] [v(d.database)]=[iter(%0, %i0|[ulocal(f.cycle.process-player, %i0)])]

@Desc XP Gain Database=Logs from the XP Gain system (weekly bonuses, votes, etc) go on this object.

&XP.SKILL.?.? XP Cost Database=1
&XP.ATTRIBUTE XP Cost Database=u(f.cost.standard, 4, %1, %2)
&XP.SKILL XP Cost Database=u(f.cost.standard, 2, %1, %2)
&XP.MERIT XP Cost Database=u(f.cost.standard, 1, %1, %2)
&F.COST.STANDARD XP Cost Database=mul(sub(%2, %1), %0)
&F.COST.DIRECT XP Cost Database=mul(%1, %0)
&D.DATA XP Cost Database=xp.
&XP.ADVANTAGE.WILLPOWER XP Cost Database=u(f.cost.single, 1, %1, %2)
&F.COST.SINGLE XP Cost Database=mul(%0, sub(%2, %1))
&F._AT_LEAST XP Cost Database=gte(add(u(f._value, %0, %1), %3), %2)

&LOG.DO XP Spend Log=[setq(t, if(gte(last(%0, |), 0), spend, unspend))][setq(r, if(gte(last(%0, |), 0), buys, refunds))][monitor([alert(+xp/%qt)] [name(first(%0, |))] %qr [if(strmatch(first(%0, |), setr(p, extract(%0, 2, 1, |))), poss(%qp), [name(%qp)]'s)] [extract(%0, 3, 1, |)] from [if(t(setr(f, extract(%0, 4, 1, |))), %qf, %(nothing%))] to [if(t(setr(t, extract(%0, 5, 1, |))), %qt, %(nothing%))] for [last(%0, |)] xp.)]
&LOG.DO.NOTES XP Spend Log=<dbref user>|<dbref target>|<statname>|<from>|<to>|<xp spent/refunded>
&LOG.GROUP XP Spend Log=A
@set XP Spend Log=INHERIT
@set XP Spend Log=SAFE !HALT
